SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ) AND (((STRING_FIELD IS NULL) AND (STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES)) AND (STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES)) OR (STRING_FIELD IS NULL) AND BOOL_FIELD = false))) AND ((((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE STRING_VALUES)) OR ((STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR ((STRING_FIELD IS NULL) AND (NOT ((STRING_FIELD IS NULL) AND (STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES)))) AND ((STRING_FIELD LIKE 'STRING_VALUES%') AND ((NOT (STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES')) OR ((STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES) OR (STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL))))))) AND (((BOOL_FIELD != true OR NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = true AND STRING_FIELD != STRING_VALUES)) OR (STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND ((BOOL_FIELD != true AND NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST DESC;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (BOOL_FIELD OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL))) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE AND NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD OR STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE 'STRING_VALUES%')) OR ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) AND ((NOT ((STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST )) OR (STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES))) OR (STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = true OR STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES)) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT DISTINCT(NUMERIC_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE NOT ((STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST )) AND ((STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES' AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NOT ((NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE)))) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE)))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((NOT (NOT ((NOT (STRING_FIELD IS NULL) AND NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)))) AND (((BOOL_FIELD = true OR NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) AND ((STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES AND NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE)))) AND (((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL AND STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE AND BOOL_FIELD != false)) OR (NOT (BOOL_FIELD)))) AND ((NOT ((NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE OR NOT (STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)))) OR (NOT ((NOT (NOT ((BOOL_FIELD = false OR STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES)))) OR (NOT ((NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE) AND ((STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES AND NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES AND NOT (BOOL_FIELD))) AND ((STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES AND NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )))))))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY STRING_FIELD_LIST ASC;
SELECT DISTINCT(NUMERIC_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((((NOT (STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES)) OR (STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) OR (STRING_FIELD LIKE 'STRING_VALUES%')) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE AND NOT (STRING_FIELD IS NULL) AND BOOL_FIELD))) OR (((BOOL_FIELD = true OR STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES%')) AND (BOOL_FIELD = true)) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST DESC;

SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL) OR (STRING_FIELD <> STRING_VALUES) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL))) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ) AND NOT (BOOL_FIELD))) OR ((BOOL_FIELD != false OR NOT (((STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES) OR (STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES)) OR (STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)))) AND (BOOL_FIELD = true) GROUP BY STRING_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NOT (((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL))) OR STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false OR (NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE))) OR ((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false OR NOT ((NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)))) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((((BOOL_FIELD OR (STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES) OR (STRING_FIELD != STRING_VALUES))) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES AND NOT (BOOL_FIELD))) OR (BOOL_FIELD != false) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE OR NOT (STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES)))) OR ((STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL) AND (NOT (BOOL_FIELD)) OR ((BOOL_FIELD AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL))) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES)))) AND (NOT ((BOOL_FIELD != false) AND (STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST )) OR (BOOL_FIELD) AND ((BOOL_FIELD != false AND STRING_FIELD IS NULL)))) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) AND ((STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE 'STRING_VALUES%' AND NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES AND NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) AND (STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST )) OR ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL))) AND ((NOT (((STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE '%STRING_VALUES') AND (STRING_FIELD != STRING_VALUES)) AND ((((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE))) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES AND BOOL_FIELD = false))))) OR (((BOOL_FIELD != true AND NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES) AND ((STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE 'STRING_VALUES%') OR (STRING_FIELD LIKE 'STRING_VALUES%'))))) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((STRING_FIELD != STRING_VALUES) OR (STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES) AND (NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE)) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST DESC;
SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL)) AND (STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE 'STRING_VALUES%')) OR (((STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES AND (((NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL))) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((((((BOOL_FIELD AND STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES%')) OR ((BOOL_FIELD OR STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES))) OR (((((BOOL_FIELD OR NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = true OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)))) OR (NOT (NOT (NOT (((BOOL_FIELD OR NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR ((BOOL_FIELD != true OR STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE '%STRING_VALUES'))))))) OR ((((BOOL_FIELD = false AND STRING_FIELD IS NULL)) AND (((STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES AND NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD OR STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES)) OR ((STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES AND NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE))) OR ((STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE 'STRING_VALUES%') OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL))))) AND ((STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES) AND ((STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE))))) OR ((NOT ((STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ) AND NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )))) OR ((BOOL_FIELD = true AND NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ))))) AND ((NOT ((((NOT (STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES)) AND (NOT ((NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD LIKE STRING_VALUES)))) OR (((NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = true OR STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST )))) AND (NOT ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL AND (STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES) AND (STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES) AND BOOL_FIELD))))) OR (NOT ((BOOL_FIELD OR STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL))))) AND (NOT ((BOOL_FIELD != false OR NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE)))) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE NOT ((NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL AND ((NOT (STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) OR (STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES)) OR (NOT (STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES)) AND BOOL_FIELD != true)) OR ((BOOL_FIELD = false OR (STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES) OR (STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES))) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES))) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT DISTINCT(NUMERIC_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((BOOL_FIELD != false AND NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE OR (STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE STRING_VALUES) OR (STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE))) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE AND (STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES) AND (STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND NOT (BOOL_FIELD))) AND (STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD != false AND NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR ((BOOL_FIELD OR STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE)) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE NOT ((STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false OR STRING_FIELD LIKE 'STRING_VALUES%')) OR (STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST )) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false OR NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE))) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (NOT (BOOL_FIELD = true)) OR (((((NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE) AND STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES AND BOOL_FIELD)) OR ((BOOL_FIELD != true AND NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE))) AND (NOT ((((BOOL_FIELD != true AND NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL))) OR (((NOT (NOT ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ))))) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)))) OR (((NOT ((BOOL_FIELD != true AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL))) AND (NOT ((BOOL_FIELD != true OR NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE))))) AND ((NOT ((BOOL_FIELD = true) OR ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)))) AND ((STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )))) OR (STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE STRING_VALUES) AND (((NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE) AND STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE '%STRING_VALUES' AND NOT (BOOL_FIELD))))))))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST ASC;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((BOOL_FIELD OR STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES)) OR (((BOOL_FIELD OR STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) OR ((BOOL_FIELD != true) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES')) OR ((BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE)))) OR (NOT (BOOL_FIELD = false)) ORDER BY STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((BOOL_FIELD OR STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES)) AND ((STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES AND NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR ((BOOL_FIELD != true AND STRING_FIELD <> STRING_VALUES)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD != false AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT DISTINCT(NUMERIC_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE NOT (((BOOL_FIELD = true OR STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD OR STRING_FIELD LIKE STRING_VALUES))) ORDER BY STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT DISTINCT(NUMERIC_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (BOOL_FIELD OR NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )))) OR ((((BOOL_FIELD OR NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )))) AND (STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT STRING_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE NOT ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST ASC;
SELECT DISTINCT(NUMERIC_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) OR (STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE 'STRING_VALUES%') GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT STRING_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL OR STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES))) AND ((NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND (NOT (NOT ((NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD <> STRING_VALUES AND BOOL_FIELD = true)))))) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND ((BOOL_FIELD OR NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL))) GROUP BY STRING_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY STRING_FIELD_LIST DESC;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((BOOL_FIELD AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE))) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ) AND STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE '%STRING_VALUES' AND BOOL_FIELD = true)) OR (STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR (((STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES AND NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE))) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES))) GROUP BY STRING_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY STRING_FIELD_LIST DESC;
SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (BOOL_FIELD AND (NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((BOOL_FIELD != true AND NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND (NOT (NOT ((STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)))))) GROUP BY STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (NOT (NOT (NOT ((((NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES) AND (STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST )) AND BOOL_FIELD = false)) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND (((STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES) OR (STRING_FIELD <> STRING_VALUES)) AND (STRING_FIELD <> STRING_VALUES)) AND (STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES))) OR ((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((NOT ((NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND (NOT (((NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)))))) AND STRING_FIELD LIKE STRING_VALUES AND BOOL_FIELD))) AND ((((STRING_FIELD IS NULL AND NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE))) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ) AND STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES AND BOOL_FIELD))))))) AND (((BOOL_FIELD = false AND (NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE))) OR (((NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE) AND STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES AND BOOL_FIELD = false))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY STRING_FIELD_LIST ASC;

SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((BOOL_FIELD != false) AND ((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL))) OR ((((NOT (STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES) AND NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL AND STRING_FIELD IS NULL AND BOOL_FIELD))) OR (((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES')) AND (((((BOOL_FIELD OR NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false AND STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES')) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ) AND BOOL_FIELD = false)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )))) OR (((NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND (NOT (BOOL_FIELD)) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND (((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE) AND ((BOOL_FIELD != true AND STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES%'))))) AND (NOT ((BOOL_FIELD != true AND NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE))))))) AND (((((STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE STRING_VALUES AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD != false AND NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR (BOOL_FIELD != false) AND ((BOOL_FIELD != true AND STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE))) OR (((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR (STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST )) AND (STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES))) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ))))) AND (BOOL_FIELD != true)) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((BOOL_FIELD AND STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) OR ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = true AND NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE)) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((BOOL_FIELD OR STRING_FIELD LIKE 'STRING_VALUES%')) OR ((BOOL_FIELD AND STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE 'STRING_VALUES%')) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE NOT ((BOOL_FIELD != true AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE)))) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL)))) ORDER BY STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (BOOL_FIELD) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE) OR ((BOOL_FIELD != true OR NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD OR STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE STRING_VALUES)) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES AND BOOL_FIELD)) AND (BOOL_FIELD != false) OR ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND (NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE))) AND (STRING_FIELD LIKE STRING_VALUES) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST ASC;
SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((BOOL_FIELD = false AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL))) AND (BOOL_FIELD) OR ((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND (NOT (BOOL_FIELD))) OR (((BOOL_FIELD = true OR STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES)) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES)) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES AND BOOL_FIELD = true)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ) AND NOT (STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES) AND NOT (BOOL_FIELD)))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY STRING_FIELD_LIST DESC;
SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ) OR STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES)) AND (BOOL_FIELD != true) OR ((((NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL) OR STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = true OR NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE))) OR ((BOOL_FIELD = true) AND ((BOOL_FIELD OR NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL))) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT DISTINCT(NUMERIC_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((BOOL_FIELD OR STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR ((NOT (STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = true OR STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES))) OR (((BOOL_FIELD OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE))) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES AND BOOL_FIELD)) OR ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST DESC;

!= false) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL))))))) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT STRING_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ) AND BOOL_FIELD)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL AND STRING_FIELD IS NULL AND BOOL_FIELD = true)) OR ((BOOL_FIELD OR NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES)) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY STRING_FIELD_LIST DESC;

SELECT STRING_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE NOT ((((BOOL_FIELD = true AND STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false OR NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE))) AND (((BOOL_FIELD AND STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) OR ((STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES) OR (NOT (STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES))))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD IS NULL)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES)) OR ((STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES') AND ((STRING_FIELD IS NULL) OR (STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE '%STRING_VALUES%'))) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES)) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST DESC;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES AND BOOL_FIELD = false)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD LIKE 'STRING_VALUES%' AND NOT (BOOL_FIELD))) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (NOT (BOOL_FIELD)) OR ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD)) AND (NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST DESC;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ) AND BOOL_FIELD = false)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD != true AND (NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL))) OR (BOOL_FIELD != true) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = true AND NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST DESC;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((((NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL) OR STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL OR (STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES) AND (NOT (STRING_FIELD <> STRING_VALUES)))) OR (NOT (STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES)) AND (NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE))) OR ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR STRING_FIELD <> STRING_VALUES)) GROUP BY STRING_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (BOOL_FIELD = false) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR ((BOOL_FIELD AND STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES)) AND ((STRING_FIELD IS NULL) AND (STRING_FIELD != STRING_VALUES)) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST ASC;

SELECT DISTINCT(NUMERIC_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE NOT ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((BOOL_FIELD != false OR STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES')) AND (BOOL_FIELD = false)) AND (NOT ((NOT (NOT ((STRING_FIELD != STRING_VALUES) AND ((NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES AND BOOL_FIELD != true)) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES))))) AND (((BOOL_FIELD = true OR STRING_FIELD IS NULL)) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)))) ORDER BY STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (NOT ((STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL AND (NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) OR (NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE))))) AND (((STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES) OR (BOOL_FIELD)) OR (NOT (((NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE) OR ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES))) OR ((((BOOL_FIELD != false AND NOT (((STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES) OR (STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES)) OR (STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES)))) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE AND (STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES%') OR (STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE '%STRING_VALUES') AND BOOL_FIELD))) AND (((NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES)) AND ((STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL AND (NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL))) OR ((BOOL_FIELD OR STRING_FIELD <> STRING_VALUES)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ) OR STRING_FIELD IS NULL))))))) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((BOOL_FIELD = false AND (((NOT ((NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE) OR (NOT ((NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL)))))) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE))) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ) OR STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL))) AND ((NOT (NOT (((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR (STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES) AND (STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES))) AND (BOOL_FIELD = false) OR (STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND (((NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE) OR STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES))))) AND (NOT (NOT ((((NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE))))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY STRING_FIELD_LIST ASC;

SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT STRING_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (BOOL_FIELD != false) AND ((BOOL_FIELD != false AND STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES)) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST DESC;
SELECT DISTINCT(NUMERIC_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((BOOL_FIELD OR NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) OR ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE))) AND ((((NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE))) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL) AND STRING_FIELD IS NULL AND BOOL_FIELD = false))) AND (((BOOL_FIELD OR NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL OR STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES)) OR ((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE))) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES)) AND (STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES) ORDER BY STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE) ORDER BY STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((BOOL_FIELD != true AND STRING_FIELD IS NULL)) OR ((((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND (STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES) OR (STRING_FIELD IS NULL))) AND ((NOT ((NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND (STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES) AND (STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES) AND BOOL_FIELD))) OR ((BOOL_FIELD != true AND NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)))) OR (((((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND (((NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE) AND STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES AND BOOL_FIELD)) OR (NOT (STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES)) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND (((BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES)))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD) OR ((BOOL_FIELD = true AND STRING_FIELD IS NULL)))) ORDER BY STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE NOT ((NOT ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD)) AND (((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) AND ((NOT (STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL) AND NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR ((BOOL_FIELD != false OR STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) AND (STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES)))) OR ((((NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE) AND STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE AND BOOL_FIELD = true)) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES)))) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (BOOL_FIELD OR NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST ASC;

SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE) OR ((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) AND (STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES) GROUP BY STRING_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT DISTINCT(NUMERIC_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE NOT (((STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES) OR (((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE) AND STRING_FIELD != STRING_VALUES AND BOOL_FIELD))) AND ((((BOOL_FIELD != true OR NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )) OR ((BOOL_FIELD AND STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )))) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL AND NOT (BOOL_FIELD)))))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY STRING_FIELD_LIST ASC;
SELECT DISTINCT(NUMERIC_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((((BOOL_FIELD = true AND NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR ((BOOL_FIELD != true AND STRING_FIELD IS NULL))) AND ((((NOT (BOOL_FIELD)) AND (STRING_FIELD LIKE STRING_VALUES)) AND ((STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL) OR ((BOOL_FIELD OR NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ))))) AND ((((STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL) AND ((BOOL_FIELD != false OR NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) OR ((STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE '%STRING_VALUES' AND NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND (STRING_FIELD != STRING_VALUES)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL))) AND ((STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD IS NULL AND BOOL_FIELD != true)))))) OR (NOT ((BOOL_FIELD OR NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE))) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((((BOOL_FIELD != true OR NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD != true OR NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE))) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL))) AND (NOT (STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE STRING_VALUES))) AND ((((BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD OR STRING_FIELD IS NULL)) OR (STRING_FIELD != STRING_VALUES) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND STRING_FIELD != STRING_VALUES))) OR (((BOOL_FIELD != true OR ((STRING_FIELD <> STRING_VALUES) AND ((STRING_FIELD <> STRING_VALUES) OR (STRING_FIELD != STRING_VALUES))) OR (STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST )))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = true OR STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) OR ((BOOL_FIELD != true AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD OR NOT (STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST )))))) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT DISTINCT(NUMERIC_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE))) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL OR STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD != true OR STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) GROUP BY STRING_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY STRING_FIELD_LIST ASC;
SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES AND NOT (BOOL_FIELD))) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL AND STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ) AND BOOL_FIELD != false))) AND ((((STRING_FIELD LIKE STRING_VALUES AND NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR (NOT (((BOOL_FIELD OR (STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE STRING_VALUES) OR (NOT ((STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES) OR (STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES))))) OR ((BOOL_FIELD = true AND STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST )))))) OR (((((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) AND (NOT (STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE STRING_VALUES)) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD LIKE STRING_VALUES AND BOOL_FIELD = true)) AND (NOT (BOOL_FIELD))) OR (NOT ((BOOL_FIELD != false AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)))) OR ((((BOOL_FIELD != true OR NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES))) AND ((STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES) AND ((BOOL_FIELD OR NOT (STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE))))))) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((BOOL_FIELD = false AND STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES')) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) OR ((BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD != false OR (STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES) OR (STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES)))) AND (NOT ((STRING_FIELD IS NULL AND NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST ASC;
SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((STRING_FIELD != STRING_VALUES AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL)) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE OR (STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES) AND (STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL))) GROUP BY STRING_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST DESC;

SELECT STRING_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ) AND STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES AND BOOL_FIELD != true)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL))) AND (((BOOL_FIELD = false OR NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((BOOL_FIELD != false AND STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE STRING_VALUES)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE OR NOT (STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES))) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES AND BOOL_FIELD)) AND (STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES')) OR ((NOT (((BOOL_FIELD = false AND STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) AND (BOOL_FIELD = true))) OR (((BOOL_FIELD OR NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT STRING_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (NOT (((((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL OR STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL))) OR ((((BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL)) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE)))) AND (((BOOL_FIELD = true AND STRING_FIELD LIKE STRING_VALUES)) AND ((STRING_FIELD LIKE STRING_VALUES AND NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) OR ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND (STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL) AND (STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = true AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL))))) AND (((BOOL_FIELD = false OR NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false OR STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) OR ((BOOL_FIELD != true AND STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES)) AND (BOOL_FIELD)))) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST DESC;

SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((BOOL_FIELD) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR ((BOOL_FIELD AND STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES)) AND (((NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE) OR STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE))) OR ((((BOOL_FIELD != true AND NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD OR NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR (((NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)))) AND (((STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ) AND NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND (NOT (((BOOL_FIELD = false AND (NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE) OR (NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE))))) AND (NOT (BOOL_FIELD)))))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY STRING_FIELD_LIST ASC;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL AND NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL))) OR ((BOOL_FIELD != false OR STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES')) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE NOT ((NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) AND (BOOL_FIELD = true) OR ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE))) AND (((NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND STRING_FIELD IS NULL AND NOT (BOOL_FIELD)))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST ASC;

SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((((BOOL_FIELD != false OR NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) AND (NOT (STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL))) OR (((((((NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) OR (STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) AND (((NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE OR NOT (STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE '%STRING_VALUES'))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD AND STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ))))) AND (NOT ((NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE) AND STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ) AND NOT (BOOL_FIELD))))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false OR STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE))) AND (((BOOL_FIELD = false OR NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE))))) OR (((BOOL_FIELD = true OR NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND (((STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES) AND (STRING_FIELD IS NULL) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE))) OR ((BOOL_FIELD AND STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES')) AND (BOOL_FIELD = true))) OR ((NOT (((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)))) OR (NOT (((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) AND ((STRING_FIELD LIKE STRING_VALUES AND NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE))))) GROUP BY STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT DISTINCT(NUMERIC_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((STRING_FIELD LIKE 'STRING_VALUES%' AND (NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD != false AND NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE))) OR (((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND (STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT DISTINCT(NUMERIC_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (STRING_FIELD <> STRING_VALUES) OR ((BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE)) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST DESC;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((BOOL_FIELD != false AND NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE AND (STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND (STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES) AND NOT (BOOL_FIELD))) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND (STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES) AND (STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES))) GROUP BY STRING_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST DESC;

SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND (STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE '%STRING_VALUES%') AND (NOT (STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL)))) AND ((NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL) AND STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE AND NOT (BOOL_FIELD)))) AND ((((NOT ((NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ) AND STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE AND BOOL_FIELD = false))) AND (((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE))) AND ((STRING_FIELD LIKE STRING_VALUES AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL)) OR ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE)))) AND (BOOL_FIELD = false)) OR ((STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE '%STRING_VALUES%') AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES)))) GROUP BY STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE) AND ((STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE STRING_VALUES) OR (STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES)) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE NOT ((((BOOL_FIELD OR NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL OR (STRING_FIELD IS NULL) AND ((STRING_FIELD IS NULL) AND (STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST )))))) AND ((((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) AND (((((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE STRING_VALUES)) AND ((NOT (STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD LIKE 'STRING_VALUES%' AND BOOL_FIELD)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE))) OR (((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((((NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL)))) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE))) AND STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES AND BOOL_FIELD = true)) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ) AND BOOL_FIELD)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL OR STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES)))) OR (((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD != false AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE))))))) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE NOT (((BOOL_FIELD != false AND STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES)) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND (STRING_FIELD IS NULL) AND (STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES))) OR ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD AND (STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE STRING_VALUES) AND (STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE 'STRING_VALUES%')))) ORDER BY STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((BOOL_FIELD != false AND NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE))) OR ((STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES AND (NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL))) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR (((((NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE) OR (NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) OR STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES)) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE 'STRING_VALUES%')) OR ((STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES) OR (STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) AND (((STRING_FIELD IS NULL) OR (STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL))) OR (((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL) AND (NOT (BOOL_FIELD))) AND (((BOOL_FIELD = true AND STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) OR ((NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE) AND STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ) AND NOT (BOOL_FIELD)))))) GROUP BY STRING_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY STRING_FIELD_LIST DESC;
SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false OR STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE STRING_VALUES)) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT STRING_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD != true OR NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE)) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY STRING_FIELD_LIST ASC;
SELECT DISTINCT(NUMERIC_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (NOT (((NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES AND BOOL_FIELD = false)) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE))) AND (((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL AND STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES AND NOT (BOOL_FIELD))) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR STRING_FIELD LIKE STRING_VALUES)) OR ((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) AND ((STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE AND NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT DISTINCT(NUMERIC_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((BOOL_FIELD = false AND (NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )))) OR ((NOT (((((BOOL_FIELD != false OR NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND (STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES') AND (STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES))) OR (NOT (STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE))) AND (NOT ((BOOL_FIELD != false AND NOT ((NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)))))) AND (NOT ((BOOL_FIELD != true AND STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL))))) OR (((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES%' AND BOOL_FIELD != false)))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR (STRING_FIELD IS NULL) OR (STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES))) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE AND BOOL_FIELD != true))) OR ((STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES) AND ((BOOL_FIELD != true AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL)) OR ((BOOL_FIELD != false AND NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = true AND NOT ((NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE))))) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR (STRING_FIELD <> STRING_VALUES)) AND (((STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE))) OR (NOT (STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST DESC;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) OR ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD != false OR (NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST DESC;
SELECT STRING_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE NOT (((NOT ((NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES))) OR ((((NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL) AND STRING_FIELD != STRING_VALUES AND BOOL_FIELD = false)) AND (NOT (BOOL_FIELD)) OR ((BOOL_FIELD = true AND NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE '%STRING_VALUES')))) OR (NOT (NOT (BOOL_FIELD)))) GROUP BY STRING_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST ASC;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (((STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES) OR (STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL) AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL AND BOOL_FIELD)) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE)) GROUP BY STRING_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST DESC;

SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((BOOL_FIELD) AND ((BOOL_FIELD OR NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE))) OR (((BOOL_FIELD = true AND STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) AND ((STRING_FIELD LIKE 'STRING_VALUES%') AND ((BOOL_FIELD != true AND NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR (BOOL_FIELD != false) AND ((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE)))) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (STRING_FIELD IS NULL) AND (NOT (BOOL_FIELD)) OR ((BOOL_FIELD AND NOT ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL))))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = true AND (STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE '%STRING_VALUES%') OR (STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES))) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT DISTINCT(NUMERIC_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE) GROUP BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST ASC;

SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST, BOOL_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (NOT (((BOOL_FIELD AND (NOT (STRING_FIELD != STRING_VALUES)) OR (STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST )))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = true AND STRING_FIELD <> STRING_VALUES)) OR ((BOOL_FIELD OR STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE)))))) OR ((((NOT ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL OR STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST )))) OR (NOT (BOOL_FIELD))) AND (NOT (BOOL_FIELD))) OR (((BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )))))) GROUP BY STRING_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST DESC;

SELECT NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST, STRING_FIELD_LIST FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (NOT (BOOL_FIELD != false)) OR ((((NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES')) AND (BOOL_FIELD)) OR (((((NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD != true AND STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL))) AND (NOT (STRING_FIELD <> STRING_VALUES)))) ORDER BY STRING_FIELD_LIST;

SELECT DISTINCT(STRING_FIELD) FROM BUCKET_NAME INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE (((BOOL_FIELD OR STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES')) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL AND BOOL_FIELD = false)) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE STRING_VALUES)) AND ((STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE 'STRING_VALUES%' AND NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE))) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )) ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST;
SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) INNER JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) LEFT JOIN BUCKET_NAME ON ( PREVIOUS_TABLE.FIELD = CURRENT_TABLE.FIELD ) WHERE NOT (((BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) AND (BOOL_FIELD = false)) GROUP BY STRING_FIELD_LIST ORDER BY NUMERIC_FIELD_LIST ASC;
